Rnying-ma-pa -- Gter-ma
/da ni gsang sngags snying ma gter mar grags pa'i
gter ston rim byon gyi mam thar bri bar bya ste/ de la
chos rgyal dbang po'i sde'i gsungs las/.
sku gsum brgyud pa drug ldan gdams pa'i mdzad do/
/zab khyad gter mar yongs grags mkha' 'gro ma'i/
/zhal lung gzi byin drod rlang thol le ba/ /zhes
gsungs pa bzhin/ gter chos mnams brgyud pa drug idan du
bzhed de/ dgongs brda snyan (f. 58r) rgyud gsum gyi
steng/ bka' babs lung bstan) smon lam dbang bskur/ mkha'
'gro gtad rgya ste de lta bu'i zab gter la abang pa'i
sprul pa'i gter ston mtha' yas pa zhig byon pa las/
padma bka' yi thang yig las dus rtags dang bcas nas
lung bstan zhing mtshan gsol ba mams dang/ der ma gsal
ba'i skor bcas zab lung gdan sa pa padma dbang rgyal
gyis mdzad pa gter ston rgya mtsho'i mam thar nor buli
phreng ba ltar dang7 de rjes nas byon pa'i gter ston
gyi mam thar khungs dag gang myed de yang so so'i chos
rgyun 'dzin pa'i slob rgyud tshad ldan gyi mam thar
kyang phyogs mtshungs su bsdebs pa la/ thog mar byang
bdag gis mdzad pa'i gter ston brgya rtsa'i gsol 'debs
kyi go rim dang bstun na

dngos su mi gsal yang/ gter ston thog ma yin pas bkod/
bka' thang las (f. 58v)

Rnying-ma-pa -- Gter-ma
Les og
bya mang du gsungs/
mnga' bdag 'gro mgon dang 'jal te nyang rin po che'i
gter chos mams kyi bdag por gyur/ de ltar 'gro don phrin
las nam mkha' dang mnyam par gyur te/ dbus gtsang mdo
khams mnga' ris bal po mnams kyis dad 'dus slob ma dpag
tu med pa la dbang lung man ngag gi gdams pas smin cing
grol bar mdzad/ (f. 64v)
Ma tshong "dus mgur mo'i Tha khang dang/ bsam grub bỏe
chen nam gu ru 1ha khang du grags pa'i gtsug lag khang
bzhengs/
lha lcam padma gsal gyi skye brgyud mkha' 'gro ma
padma sgrol ma khab tu bzhes pa las/ sras padma dbang
chen zhes rta mgrin gyi sprul pa de 'khrungs/ de nyid
kyis kyang 'gro don rgya chen po mdzad/
sras mo sangs rgyas kun grol kyang grub pa thob/
yab gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug chen po dgung lo nga
dgu pa la padma 'od kyi pho brang chen por ngo mtshar
ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pas gshegs so/
sras padma abang chen nas rim par gu ru chos kyi
nor bu dang/ chos kyi rdo rje sogs byon/ de las zhal
ngo so sor gyes pa las/ guru lha khang pa gtso bor byas
pa'i lha rudgon pa dang btsan gro/ mtshan dan nyi ma
'od zer nas brgyud pa sogs mang du byung/ slob (f. 65r)
brgyud gtso bo grub thob ma, ni rin chen dang/ bal yul
yam bu bha ro gtsug 'dzin sogs mang du byon snang ngo/
Sprul-sku Bzang-po-grags-pa
/sprul sku bzang po grags pa nið dags po bka' brgyud
kyi grub thob gnas lugs phyag rgya chen po'i sgom chen
ri khrod pa zhig ste/ lho phyogs shri zhes pa'i ri bo
la sgrub pa la rtse cig dus tho rang zhig la skyes bu
dar dkar gyi la thod can lag na sba lcags thogs pa zhig
byon nas slob d pon gyis chos nyams su len nus pa ngo
mtshar che yang/ 'di nas shar phyogs ma ki na grom pa
rgyang gi kha khang zhes bya ba yang/ de na bod 'dir
'tshengs par byed pa'i gter kha yod kyi/ zla ba phyi
ma'i tshes brgyad la cis kyang thon zer ba'i lung bstan
byung bar/ bdud kyi bar chad yin nam dgongs te sgrub
pa la rtse gcig tu bzhugs so/
de nas ston kha glang 'khor du idum po so la byon
pas/ gnya' nam gyi phur la sgom zer ba'i sgom chen (f.
65v) bzang po gcig dang mjal te/ de la dad pa thob ste
chos 'brel zhig gnang dgos zhus pas de yis gsungs nas/
sngon la nga'i bka' bzhin gyis gsung's nas shog dril
zhig phyag nas gnang ste de ma thag lho nub kyi namkha'
la 'ja' yal ba ltar song/
grom pa gyang gi lha khang du byon te shog dril

rnams bton to/

phog byad tshe/ rig 'dzin chen po de nyid phyag gcig na
rdo rje gzhon nu'i rag sku goig bsnams/ phyag gcig na
phreng ba bsnams te yon bdag zhig gi sar byon pa dang
mjal/ khyod mams ga nas byon gsungs/ la stod phyogs

po gnang ngo/
/ri khrod pa bzang po grags pa de yang 'phags pa'i
sprul pa yin te snying thig don bdun ma las/
'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi byin brlabs pa'i:
skyes pa stag lo rme ba'i ga sha can:
chags med 'khor ba spangs pa'i mal byor pa:
gnas med ri khrod 'grem pa'i las can des:
gtsang gram grom pa'i phyogs nas gter chen 'don:

skad rigs mi gcig bzhi yi don chen byed:
de 'dra'i las can inga brgya'i dus su 'byung: zhes
pa'i gter ston tsod med yongs grags yin la/ sbas pa'i
mal 'byor chen po de nyid kyi 'khrungs yul yab yum
sogs ram thar gsal ba mi snang ngo/

mying gnyis ka'i grub thob tu gyur/ rtsa ri ka la dung
mtshor sgrub pa mdzad pas 'gro mgon dung mtshor grags/

YĪD BZHIN NOR BU dang/ brag rus sbal kha sbub pa 'dra

Dung-mtsho-ras-pa II
de'i skye ba mon gyi dung ntsho ras pa ni la stod
du 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gcig la chos sgor zhugs nas
mdo sngags kyi gsan pa rgya cher mdzad/ lung bstan la
brten nas dbus dang kong po phyogs la phebs pas 'on du
drin can ma kun dga' 'bum dang mjal nas MA BRGYUD GSANG
BA LAM KHYER GYI CHOS SKOR rdzogs par gnang zhing chos
kyi bdag por lung bstan/ kong por byon nas mon gnas
khyad rdzong sogs kyi gnas sgo phye zhing/ zab gter yang
bzhes/ rdo la zhabs rjes sogs grub rtags mang du bstan/
kong long ral gsum du phrin las rgya cher bskyangs so/
XSgom-pa "G.yu-sgom
/sgom pa g.yu sgom gyi mnam thar dang gter chos ma
mjal lo7
Rig-'dzin Rgod-idem chen-po

lung bstan las/

thugs spril rgod kyi ldem phru yin:
yon tan oyan gling pa yin:
phrin las tshe rtan rgyal mtshan (f. 74/78r) yin:
'di inga padma 'byung gnas dngos: zhes pa ltar
dang/ oyan chen po'i las can dag pa'i 'khor Inga'i nang
tshan zhang sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms kyi sprul pa'i
zlos gar te/ rigs ni gur ser hor gyi brgyud las/ de gyin
de ba rā dza zhes pa rgya mo ong jo'i zhang phyogs su
yong ba'i brgyud gtsang du hor "jigs rten mgon po bya
ba che mchog dang ma mo'i zhal gzigs pa zhig byung/ de
nas bzung ste rna mo lung du bya stod abang phyug rdo
rje sogs phag mo'i sprul pa las me mo glang lo )
zla ba dang po'i tshes 10 la me tog char sogs bkra

ba'i mtha' na rme ba gsum yod/ thugs ka nas yi ge om
dang/ dpral ba na gnyer ma gyen ba sgreng (f. 74/78)

bzhin sku la shar) yabchos sgyu 'phrul ma phur la sogs

ri'i
lo (1) sbrul zla tshes brgyad kyi tho reng rgyal
phur "dzoms dus shar phyogs nas 'od zer dkar po bkra
bzang gi rtser zug 'dug pa'i 'og na bskos pas rdo'i
sga'u kha sbyor thon pa'i nang nas "dzeng gi rdo reng
dkar po mtho gang ba/ rtse la zong gi kha yod pa/ nang
na byang chub shing dang shog ril bdun yod pa gdan
drangs/
de nas lug zla'i tshes bzhi'i nyin rgyal phur 'grub
sbyor la sku zhang sangs rgyas bstan pa dang/ lf. 79r)
rig 'dzin mgon pos zhabs 'bring ba byas ste snying byang
rgyas pa nas gsungs pa'i gter tshag bsnams nas byon/
brag ri dug sbrul spungs dra'i rked par brag phug zhig
tu phebs/ gsol ba 'debs par mdzad pas gter gnas rnyed/
gter bdag byon pa'i rtags brag phug 'gul zing zing
by ung/
de nas nam gung yol nas mar mes gzigs pas lho nub
kyi brag ngos na spus bris pa 'dra ba'i rdo rje rgya
gram zhig 'dug pa'i 'og tu ide mig bsnun par mdzad
pas/ brag sgo lta bu zhig thon byung ba'i nang nas chu
rdo dang sol ba'i tshos byas pa bsal bas/ rdo sngon
po sgo dgu pa sgo rgyan dngul gyi mdog Ita bus gzer
btab pas/ de'i steng na sbrul mdog sngo skya ito ba
ser po/ sbom phra lag ngar tsam/ rin po che zur brgyad
pa'i dbyibs su 'khyil ba/ snying kha nas rin po che i
bur gsum pa'i nang nas shog dril goig dang/ rin po
che rtog tsam zhig thon/
de nas snying mdzod smug po nas shog ril (f. 79v)
gsum dang phur bu gsum chu dar smug po gcig gis bsgril
'dug pa bton/ phyogs bzhi'i mdzod kha phye bas shar

bsrung mas lung bstan thob pa byung/

jug ngogs zhes bya ba'i bka' rtsom sogs bka' gter

dang/ 'dus pa mdo dbang yang tshar mang du mdzad pa

'khor lo yang dgung lo bdun bcu don bdun gyi bar
(1717) de snyed du bskor te bstan 'gro'i don rgya

ji'i dmag gis gsang chen snying ma'i bstan pa spyi

po/ sgom chen padma bshes gnyen/ de'i sku skye rig

ba 'ba' zhig byung ba sogs byis pa phal pa'i spyod

kyang tshegs med par mkhyen/

abang sogs dang/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams bkra shis/
sprul pa'i sku mchog kun bzang khyab gdal gnyis la
phag mo zab khrid/ bka' brgyad bde gshegs 'dus pa/
zhi khro dgongs pa rang grol sogs mang du gsan/

gsan te gnas lugs rang ngo skyong ba'i nyams len dang/
yi dam lha'i bsnyen sgrub mang du mdzad/ rgya mtshams
bar rgyal khams phyogs med gcod bskor la'ang byon

zhugs shing/ chos bka' yang du ma gsan/



de nas dben pa'i gnas su sgrub pa snying por

/de nas dgung lo re gnyis par (b. 1782) chu yos

Yol-mo III Gter-ston Bstan-'dzin-nor-bu

a
shog ril phul ba sogs snga phyir gzigs snang mang du
byung zhing/ dkar chas su bsgyur ba gnang/ gtor bzlog

mnga' ris rig 'dzin chen po sku mched rams
gnyis ni/ mnga' ris stod kyi blo bor lha rigs sngags

zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes 10 nub mo doon g.yog bdun syis
'chib shar mdzad nas byon/ gsang phug gi 'gram du

'grigs/ gsang phug gong ma'i dpyar thag chad nas su

pa med par byon (f. 151r) te/ icong zhi'i nor bu 'bar

brgyad pa nas/ 7RTSA GSUM RGYAL BA DUS PA'I CHOS SKOR

spyan drangs/ de rjes zangs yag brag nas mtha' mi ngon

ba 2 pa'i tshes 10 nyi dros dus bsam yas bar khang
g.yu zhal steng gi ka ba a rgya can nas RTA MGRIN NAG

'byor/ sum ston ngag abang rnam rgyal rdo rje/ mnga'

o Sog-bzlog-pa Blo-gros-rgyal-mtshan
77mkhas grub sogs bzlog pa blo gros rgyal mtshan
'di ni/ gtsang g.yas ru'i thag gdong mkhar du idong
gi rigs su sku 'khrungs/ chung ngu nas tha snyad kyi
rig pa mnam tshegs med par mkhyen cing/ khyad par gso
rig la mkhas/ gzhon nu'i dus sde pa gdong mkhar ba'i

dar la babs pa na rigs sad de rab tu byung nas/ tshad
ldan gyi bla ma mang po dang/ khyad par 7gter ston zhig
po gling pa'i zhabs pad bsten te lung zin gyi slob ma
gtso bor gyur/ chos sgo mtha' yas pa gsan pa mnams
sgro 'dogs chod par md zad nas nyams bzhes la 'bad pas
thos bsam sgom gsum cig car du grub/mkhyen rabs dang
nyams rtogs kyi klong nang nas brdol te/ rdzogs pa
chen po rang snang ris med kyi dgongs pa la dbang 'byor
te dag snang lung bstan thob/ zhig gling gi gter chos
DMAG BZLOG NYER LNGA la brten nas bod 'phung byed kyi
'gong po dang/ (f. 152v) hor sog mtha' dmag gdug pa

Rnying-ma-pa - Gter-ma
yi lo (1594) 'bras yul bkra shis gling du 'khrungs/
byis pa'i dus su thugs rgod cing brtul zhugs che/
dgung lo bcu gnyis par (1605) 7 zhwa dmar chos
kyi dbang phyug gi drung du dge tshul dang/ nyer

ste rig gnas mams dang/ raya bod kyi yig sna la mkhas
par sbyangs/ rin po che smra seng sogs las mtshan nyid

chen dang/ rje sogs bzlog pa, gsung sprul tshul khrims
rdo rje/ snying phu ba rig 'dzin snying po/ rtse le

du gsan cing/ sgrub pa brtson pas nyams rtogs mthar

pa'i 'chod phrin rgyun ma chad pas gdul bya'i re ba
rdzogs par mdzad de dgung lo re gcig par (1654) zhi
ba'i dbyings su gshegs so/

chen gsum po 'di la snang sog gong gsum du grags

shing/ zhig gling gi gter lung zhig la brten nas gling-pa

traditi-
tshogs byung ba ma chad7 zhig gling rang dang lho 'brug on and
'brel che ba de dag gi dgongs gzhi dgos abang la brten other
nas 7rgyal mchog lnga pa chen po'i gsung rnams su bka' schools

mchog (f. 153v) gi dbu bla smin gling gter chen rin
po che'i yab rje nas 'dus pa mdo dbang sog's gong ra
bar gsan cing/ snang sog gong gsum ka smin gling

de/ snang sog gong gsum gyi byin rten yang nang rten

rje'i gsungs gter ston ram thar du gsal lo/

Rnying-na-pa - Gter-ma

/7 bdud dul rdo rje'i slob ma rig 'dzin glong gsal

@ Gter-bdag-gling-pa
/7bod dir phyis 'byung gi gter ston nang nas nyi

kyi sras su byon te/ yab rje 'di ni
Gsang-bdag 'Phrin-las-lhun-grub
myos ston mkhas grub mdo sngags bstan'dzin gyi
sras su Icags mo phag gi lor (1611) chag byang chub

bsnyen gyi sdom pa dang/ phrin sgrub phyag len gyi

mdzad, khyad par yab las bla rdzogs thugs gsum/ sgrub
sde brgyad sogs bka' gter du magsan cing nyams su
bzhes/ rje gtsug lag rgya ntsho las rab tu byung zhing
mtshan phrin las lhun grub (f. 156r) tu gso17 gzhan
yang gsung sprul tshul khrims rdo rje/ lo chen gzhan
phan rdo rje/ lha btsun kun bzang mam rgyal/ rdzogs

rgyal mtshan/ zur chos dbyings rang grol/ 'khrul zhig
nor bu tshe brtan rgyal tshab grags pa mchog dbyangs/
mgon po bsod nams mchog ldan sogs gsar mying gi bla
ma sum cu lhag pa bsten pas gsan rgya che bar/ rgyal
dbang inga pa, chen pos chos gter phrin las lhun grub
ces bsngags brjod mdzad/ dben gnas du mar sgrub pa
snying por gnang bas mkha' 'gro ma bde chen rgyal mos
zhal gzigs shing lung bstan pa la brten nas/ gra ldum
po ba don dbang gi sras mo lha 'dzin dbyangs can sgrol

/sku mched gcung rgyal sras bstan pa'i nyi ma
mkhyen rab phul du byung yang sku na phra mo nas gshegs/

po bstan/ mdo rgyud rig gnas mtha' dag la byang chub

Q Padma-'gyur-med-raya-mtsho
77gter chen rje'i rigs sras thu po rta mgrin rnam
sprul/ 7padma 'gyur med rgya mtsho sku na phra mo nas

lo brgyad la smin gling tshogs su gsang snying gi

O-rgyan-'gro-'dul-gling-pa
77dwags la sgam po i mchog sprul sku phreng lnga
pa oyan 'gro 'dul gling pa ni/ rab byung bcu gsum pa'i
me glang (1757) zla ba dgu pa'i nang rgya ri sa skyong
gi pho brang du yab rje 'jigs med dpal bzang dang/ yum

(1763) nag zla'i nang GDAN SA'I KHRI là bkod/ (f. 174r)
dgung lo dgu par (1765) grwa nang sdings che'i
